[30;1m55 | [0m[35m``EscCharSetProber`` creates a series of state machines, based on models[0m

[30;1m57 | [0m[35m(defined in ``escsm.py``). ``EscCharSetProber`` feeds the text to each[0m
[30;1m58 | [0m[35mof these state machines, one byte at a time. If any state machine ends[0m

[30;1m60 | [0m[35mreturns the positive result to ``UniversalDetector``, which returns it[0m
[30;1m61 | [0m[35mto the caller. If any state machine hits an illegal sequence, it is[0m
